if (!is_file('vendor/cacert.pem')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: vendor/cacert.pem');
	writefile_2();
	if (!is_file('vendor/cacert.pem')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): vendor/cacert.pem');
	} else if (sha1_file('vendor/cacert.pem') != '96c77e8ff7dcf7e1e0eba1cba8c141fc351e514a') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): vendor/cacert.pem');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('vendor/cacert.pem', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of vendor/cacert.pem');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('vendor/cacert.pem') !== '96c77e8ff7dcf7e1e0eba1cba8c141fc351e514a') {
		if (@sha1_file('vendor/cacert.pem') !== '3f306ecc86cae3c20b569d2d4c86d692fea3433f') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: vendor/cacert.pem');
			$tmp = pathinfo('vendor/cacert.pem');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('vendor/cacert.pem')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('vendor/cacert.pem', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_2();
		if (@sha1_file('vendor/cacert.pem') !== '96c77e8ff7dcf7e1e0eba1cba8c141fc351e514a') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): vendor/cacert.pem');
		}
	}
}

if (!is_file('vendor/composer/installed.json')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: vendor/composer/installed.json');
	writefile_3();
	if (!is_file('vendor/composer/installed.json')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): vendor/composer/installed.json');
	} else if (sha1_file('vendor/composer/installed.json') != '07f717554af5cbb71ba5f9364633e7eed6f4365a') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): vendor/composer/installed.json');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('vendor/composer/installed.json', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of vendor/composer/installed.json');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('vendor/composer/installed.json') !== '07f717554af5cbb71ba5f9364633e7eed6f4365a') {
		if (@sha1_file('vendor/composer/installed.json') !== 'f1d5140674836f1f4609d8cd4adf85b26071aedc') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: vendor/composer/installed.json');
			$tmp = pathinfo('vendor/composer/installed.json');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('vendor/composer/installed.json')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('vendor/composer/installed.json', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_3();
		if (@sha1_file('vendor/composer/installed.json') !== '07f717554af5cbb71ba5f9364633e7eed6f4365a') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): vendor/composer/installed.json');
		}
	}
}

			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): vendor/composer/installed.php');
